During my visits I have witnessed the cook yelling at the cashier for not taking the order correctly and not knowing who's order is who's during a busy time. Cashier was frustrated, chef was frustrated and we all (about 5 of us) waiting to get our order were frustrated.  Today was the last straw. I called ahead for 1 bowl, was told 10 minutes, I waited 15 minutes (based on my past experience), get there and they have absolutely no record of my order. Again, chef being very short with both cashiers. Yep, two of them.  (probably as frustrated as I was). As I told them I could not wait, I turn around to meet the faces of 2 other customers who have been waiting 20 minutes and more frustrated than I. I refuse to support them until they make some changes and actually make training all the new faces a priority. Once is an accident, twice maybe a fluke but three or more is simply neglect. < review>
Been going here nearly every weekday in the afternoon since late March 2019 due to strictly monitoring my caloric intake. Food is good and consistent; staff is nice, courteous, and professional. Water is filtered and cold, even without ice. Patrons here can sometimes be messy (like most places), but staff keeps things clean. I've been served by the owner a few times, who is kind and jovial.

As to what I order, I religiously order 1 chicken & veggie bowl with brown rice and no green onions. I top it with hot sauce, triple hot sauce, jalapenos, and black pepper. (Yes, I like it hot, even as tears start coming out out.) Staff knows me by sight now and knows what I'll be ordering.

I hate avocado, but they serve it here and people order it frequently enough so I guess it's good. I've also had the beef bowl, the half & half, and plate-size portions before. All are good; the orange slice and salad on the plate are simple but surprisingly refreshing, which is kinda' Flame Broiler in a nutshell.

This place is my peaceful little lunch getaway from work and generally the highlight of my work day. Parking in the plaza is pretty bad but I walk here for lunch anyway!

Protip: The restroom code is printed out on your receipt, but I'm assuming no one notices that. Staff will readily give the code to customers when asked anyway.<//review>

< Review>
Hal's Auto Care went above and beyond for me recently.  I had multiple service maintenance items performed on my Honda Accord recently.  However, when picking up my car, there was a serious problem.  The engine sounded horrible.  They offered a loaner vehicle and took it back in the shop.  They spent the next few days troubleshooting what might have gone wrong.  Methodically, they began to rule out their work as they analyzed the car.  They even called my previous Honda dealer where I got my car serviced to try to identify the problem.  After about a week they found the problem to be the timing belt had jumped 5 teeth on the rea cam.  It turned out to be a failed hydraulic tensioner.  The thing is, they didn't do any work on that or anything related so it was unlikely to be due to their fault.  But because it happened on their lot they took ownership of the issue.  They ended up fixing it and working out a very reasonable deal.  They also did not charge me for all the diagnosis time for troubleshooting.  This was a very unfortunate coincidence that they took ownership of and it really proved how great they are.  Their team is humble and trust worthy.  I highly recommend them.</Review>

This homely restaurant has delicious Italian food as if it's a restaurant in Rome. There is usual a dinner rush, so it is wise to make a reservation. The service is excellent, and the waiters and waitresses are very accommodating. One important thing of note is to avoid the first table at the front of the restaurant. <userid>100723131934978308206< /userid>< username>
Jay Mehta<//username>
< date>
1467093371855< /date>
< Rating>
4< /Rating>
<Text>This is probably one of the finest Italian restaurants we have been so far. We went there for a dinner and had a great time, of course at the cost of a big hole in our pocket.

Food:
We had Bruschetta, Ravioli Di Spinachi, a classic Tiramisu and the Dessert of the day (Cannoli) and none of them disappointed. Bruschetta were good - nothing too facy or overdone but just right. Ravioli Di Spinachi was amazing. Filling was good and the parmesan sauce was brilliant. What blew away our mind was Tiramisu which was absolutely delicious. It is a must try and a disappointment if you're planning Italian desserts and not ordering Tiramisu. Cannoli was good but not so much that it goes into the list of Dessert of the Day.
Overall, the food was quite above the benchmark but it is quite heavily priced too, so be ready to sign a big check at the end.

Ambiance:
The place is a little dark. Perhaps a little more bright light will give it a better feeling. Not much cramped and very comfortable seating - more like restaurants which are meant for fine dining. Given that we went on a weekday night, it wasn't much crowded.

Service:
The service was good and quick. The food took reasonable time to come. But if you're in a rush, this restaurant is not for you. The staff is good overall - no bad experience as such.

Overall, if you're in San Francisco, this restaurant is a must try if you want to taste some real good Italian.<//Text><pics>None<//pics><resp>None</resp><GmapID>0x8085808de181fbb3:0x3b273ce2003bcbd< /GmapID></record></dataset><record>

<user_id>108653813057118053031</user_id><user_name>Barbara Chin<//user_name><Date>1521036646145<//Date><Rate>4< /Rate><Review>I've only come here twice and both times only to get the same thing: the gluten-free Carrot Walnut Tea Cake. I was amazed to find that EVERYTHING here is vegan (they don't advertise that really), though they only have a couple of items that are gluten-free (aside from their chocolates). The first time I came, they only had the tea cake and were out of everything else gluten-free, and the second time I came, there was a gluten-free quiche but I wasn't hungry enough for a whole quiche, so I got the tea cake again.

The tea cake is delicious and you wouldn't really know it was vegan and gluten-free unless someone told you (at least, I don't think so). Great texture and not at all dry or crumbly. Speedy checkout and there are a fair number of tables to sit at, but most of them were occupied when I was there both times.

Absolutely love it here. We had the Twinkie, cocoa, cappuccino, and a pour over Ethiopian. All we're delicious, made with intention and presented in a lovely way. The atmosphere is great for hanging out, doing work, chatting... We saw a huge table with a few families gathering and several people alone on laptops, people reading and people getting coffee to go. If we lived in the area, we'd definitely pick this as a regular spot. Also, if you're not sure about a dairy-less latte, or cappuccino, I'd recommend trying your drink with Oat Milk. The food & coffee are great. I used to like picking up pastries for dessert from Timeless. But for some reason, every time I go I am met with the most extremely unpleasant attitudes. Workers that were smiling & laughing with the customer in front of me become extremely apathetic & disinterested when they see me. Like they literally cannot wait for me to go.

I've come in on my own & with others, and this attitude is always the case. I am not sure what I did; I always tip and I've never stayed there for longer than it took to finish my coffee. Customer service is very hard work, so I don't like to get down on service workers; but regular rudeness that others don't seem to get is highly suspicious when it's coming from gentrifiers.

My recommendation is if you want to try this place out, send in a white hipster to place the order for you. I've never had food from here I didn't like, so it's a real shame they have issues with *some* of their customers.</Review>

<Rate>3< /Rate>< review>
Short list of teas, but good ones. Great ambiance & friendly service. Have not tried their sweets, but they look very good.
Since I am a comcast user, I have access to their network of xfinity wifi hotspots, but unfortunately the signal at Timeless Coffee is worst than bad, providing a crappy connection - and they do not offer their own wifi, a lack of service that took one star off my review.
Last time I went here it was about 5pm on a weekday, and it was not crowded, perfect for doing some work on my computer - but, it would have been better if they offered wifi...
Chairs are comfortable, large windows bring great natural light to tables, made of metal and heavy wood, which makes them very stable. You can feel the care the owners have put into creating a great coffee.<//review>
